==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The null check is broken since it will throw a NullPointerException itself. It is likely that you used || instead of && or vice versa.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// should be &&
public class Foo {
    Object buz;
    Object bar(Object list) {
        if (list != null || !list.equals(buz)) {
            return list;
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

        ——ASTVariableDeclaratorId (declared variable name = 'buz')
    ——ASTMethodDeclaration (method name = 'bar')
      ——ASTModifierList
      ——ASTClassOrInterfaceType (method return type = 'Object')
      ——ASTFormalParameters (size = 1)
        ——ASTFormalParameter
          ——ASTModifierList

              ——ASTVariableAccess (referenced variable name = 'list')

                ——ASTArgumentList (size = 1)
                  ——ASTVariableAccess (referenced variable name = 'buz')
          ——ASTBlock
            ——ASTReturnStatement
              ——ASTVariableAccess (referenced variable name = 'list')

Note, when there are consecutive method calls, the last call is at the upper level of the syntax tree.

The checker code framework(you must conform to):
```java

    public rule_name() {
        super(node1_Of_AST_to_visit.class, node2_Of_AST_to_visit.class, ...);
    }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
    @Override
    public Object visit(node2_Of_AST_to_visit node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
    ...
}
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    if (!infixExpression.getImage().equals("&&")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression expression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);
        
        if (expression != null) {
            ASTConditionalOrExpression conditionalOrExpression = expression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConditionalOrExpression.class);
            if (conditionalOrExpression != null) {
                // Check if the conditional or expression involves a null check and a method call
                boolean nullCheck = false;
                boolean methodCall = false;
                for (int i = 0; i < conditionalOrExpression.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
                    Node child = conditionalOrExpression.jjtGetChild(i);
                    if (child instanceof ASTEqualityExpression) {
                        ASTEqualityExpression equalityExpression = (ASTEqualityExpression) child;
                        if (equalityExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                            nullCheck = true;
                        }
                    } else if (child instanceof ASTPrimaryExpression) {
                        ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = (ASTPrimaryExpression) child;
                        if (primaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodDeclaration.class)) {
                            methodCall = true;
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // If both a null check and method call are present in the conditional or expression, add a violation
                if (nullCheck && methodCall) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
编译是否通过？
False

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    // Check if the operator is logical OR
                    if (infixExpression.getOperator().equals("||")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (isBrokenNullCheck(methodCall)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isBrokenNullCheck(ASTMethodCall methodCall) {
        ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
        if (unaryExpression != null) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                return true;
            }
        }

        // Check for method call on null check
        ASTMethodCall parentMethodCall = methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (parentMethodCall != null) {
            ASTMethodCall childMethodCall = parentMethodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (childMethodCall != null && childMethodCall.getImage().equals(methodCall.getImage())) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) || infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class))) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall != null && 
               (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null || 
                methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                checkMethodCall(infixExpression, data, node);
            }
            for (ASTInfixExpression childInfixExpression : infixExpression.findDescendantsOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
                if (childInfixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                    checkMethodCall(childInfixExpression, data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkMethodCall(ASTInfixExpression infixExpression, Object data, ASTIfStatement node) {
        ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
        if (methodCall != null && methodCall.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression parentInfixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) methodCall.jjtGetParent();
            if (parentInfixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            checkMethodCall(methodCall, node, data, infixExpression);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkMethodCall(ASTMethodCall methodCall, ASTIfStatement node, Object data, ASTInfixExpression infixExpression) {
        if (methodCall != null) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression != null) {
                ASTMethodCall siblingMethodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstParentOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (siblingMethodCall != null && siblingMethodCall != methodCall && siblingMethodCall.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(1).jjtGetParent().jjtGetChild(1).equals(infixExpression.jjtGetChild(0))) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        else if(infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
            ASTInfixExpression secondInfixExpression = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if(secondInfixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) && secondInfixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = secondInfixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = secondInfixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if(variableAccess != null && methodCall != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            } else if ("&&".equals(infixExpression.getOperator())) {
                Node firstExpression = infixExpression.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (firstExpression instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                    ASTInfixExpression firstInfixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) firstExpression;
                    if ("==".equals(firstInfixExpression.getOperator()) && firstInfixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null || 
                    (infixExpression.getImage().equals("&&") && variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class).getImage().equals("=="))) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
            // Additional condition to check for the case where null is checked with &&
            else if (infixExpression.getImage().equalsIgnoreCase("&&")) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null || infixExpression.getImage().equals("&&")) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) 
                    && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class) 
                && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
            ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
            if (nullLiteral.getFirstParentOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = nullLiteral.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            ASTInfixExpression nullCheck = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = nullCheck.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && nullCheck.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
                ASTInfixExpression comparison = nullCheck.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (comparison.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                    ASTVariableAccess comparisonVariable = comparison.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (comparisonVariable != null && comparisonVariable.getImage().equals(variableAccess.getImage())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkBrokenNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkBrokenNullCheck(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression expr = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTExpression.class);
        if (expr != null) {
            ASTConditionalAndExpression andExpr = expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConditionalAndExpression.class);
            if (andExpr != null) {
                ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpr = andExpr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
                if (primaryExpr != null) {
                    ASTPrimaryPrefix prefix = primaryExpr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryPrefix.class);
                    if (prefix != null && prefix.usesThisModifier()) {
                        ASTVariableDeclaratorId varId = primaryExpr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
                        if (varId != null && varId.hasImageEqualTo("null")) {
                            ASTEqualityExpression equalityExpr = andExpr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTEqualityExpression.class);
                            if (equalityExpr != null && equalityExpr.isNotEquals()) {
                                ASTBooleanLiteral booleanLiteral = equalityExpr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBooleanLiteral.class);
                                if (booleanLiteral != null) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkBrokenNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        checkBrokenNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkBrokenNullCheck(Object node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = ((net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null
                && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)
                || infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if ((methodCall != null && methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null)
                || (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null)) {
                addViolation(data, (net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node);
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpressionChild = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpressionChild != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpressionChild.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = infixExpressionChild.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
                ASTBooleanLiteral booleanLiteral = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTBooleanLiteral.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && nullLiteral != null && booleanLiteral != null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        processNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        processNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void processNode(Node node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)
                    || variableAccess.getImage().equals("boo"))) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForBrokenNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        checkForBrokenNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForBrokenNullCheck(Object node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = ((net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            ASTEqualityExpression equalityExpression = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTEqualityExpression.class);
            if (equalityExpression != null && equalityExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = equalityExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class) != null) {
                    addViolation(data, (net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            ASTInfixExpression firstInfixExpression = infixExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            ASTInfixExpression secondInfixExpression = infixExpression.getLastChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);

            if (firstInfixExpression != null && secondInfixExpression != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess firstVariableAccess = firstInfixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                ASTVariableAccess secondVariableAccess = secondInfixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);

                if (firstVariableAccess != null && secondVariableAccess != null && firstVariableAccess.getImage().equals(secondVariableAccess.getImage())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && "null".equals(variableAccess.getImage())) {
                    ASTInfixExpression sibling = variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                    if (sibling != null && sibling.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                        ASTVariableAccess siblingAccess = sibling.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                        if (siblingAccess != null && !siblingAccess.getImage().equals("null")) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
```

public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) || infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class))) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && !variableAccess.getImage().equals("null")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            ASTInfixExpression leftExpression = infixExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            ASTInfixExpression rightExpression = infixExpression.getLastChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            
            if (leftExpression != null && rightExpression != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccessLeft = leftExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccessRight = rightExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                
                if (variableAccessLeft != null && variableAccessRight != null) {
                    if (variableAccessLeft.getImage().equals(variableAccessRight.getImage())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTIfStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkForBrokenNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        checkForBrokenNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForBrokenNullCheck(Node node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class) != null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression expression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTExpression.class);
        if (expression != null) {
            ASTConditionalExpression conditionalExpression = expression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTConditionalExpression.class);
            if (conditionalExpression != null) {
                ASTEqualityExpression equalityExpression = conditionalExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTEqualityExpression.class);
                if (equalityExpression != null) {
                    ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = equalityExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
                    if (primaryExpression != null) {
                        ASTPrimaryPrefix primaryPrefix = primaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryPrefix.class);
                        if (primaryPrefix != null && primaryPrefix.usesThisModifier()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if(infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        checkNode(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkNode(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        
        if(infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if(variableAccess != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
     
        while (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) || infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTFieldAccess.class)) {
                ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = infixExpression.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
                if (unaryExpression != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            infixExpression = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            // Check for method call
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }

            // Check for method reference
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodReference.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }

            // Check for field access
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTFieldAccess.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }

            // Check for constructor call
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                checkForViolation(node, infixExpression, data);
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTFieldAccess.class)) {
                checkForViolation(node, infixExpression, data);
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class)) {
                checkForViolation(node, infixExpression, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForViolation(ASTIfStatement node, ASTInfixExpression infixExpression, Object data) {
        ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
        if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getNameDeclaration() != null && variableAccess.getNameDeclaration().getName().equals("list") && variableAccess.getUsages().size() > 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;

public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkInfixExpression(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkInfixExpression(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
            if (nullLiteral != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null) {
                    if (variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null || variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTFieldAccess.class) != null || variableAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class) != null) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && isInfixExpressionBroken(infixExpression)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isInfixExpressionBroken(ASTInfixExpression infixExpression) {
        if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                return variableAccess != null;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) || 
        infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class))) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class)) {
                ASTArrayAccess arrayAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class);
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = arrayAccess.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("arr")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTIfStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTConditionalExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkCondition(node.getCondition(), data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConditionalExpression node, Object data) {
        checkCondition(node.getCondition(), data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkCondition(Node node, Object data) {
        if (node instanceof ASTEqualityExpression) {
            checkEqualityExpression((ASTEqualityExpression) node, data);
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            checkCondition(node.jjtGetChild(i), data);
        }
    }

    private void checkEqualityExpression(ASTEqualityExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() != 2) {
            return;
        }
        Node first = node.jjtGetChild(0);
        Node second = node.jjtGetChild(1);
        if (first instanceof ASTNullLiteral && isNullCheckBroken(second)
                || second instanceof ASTNullLiteral && isNullCheckBroken(first)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
    }

    private boolean isNullCheckBroken(Node node) {
        if (node instanceof ASTPrimaryExpression && node.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1) {
            Node suffix = node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (suffix instanceof ASTPrimarySuffix && ((ASTPrimarySuffix) suffix).isArrayDereference()) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class)) {
                ASTArrayAccess arrayAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class);
                if (arrayAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = arrayAccess.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("arr")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTIfStatement.class);
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        checkNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkNullCheck(Object node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = ((net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            ASTNullLiteral nullCheck = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
            ASTVariableAccess variableCheck = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (nullCheck != null && variableCheck != null) {
                int nullPosition = infixExpression.jjtGetChildIndex(nullCheck);
                int variablePosition = infixExpression.jjtGetChildIndex(variableCheck);
                if (Math.abs(nullPosition - variablePosition) == 1) {
                    addViolation(data, (net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        checkNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        checkNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkNullCheck(Object node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = ((net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        // Check if the parent node is an infix expression
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            // Check if the infix expression has a null literal
            ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
            if (nullLiteral != null) {
                // Check if the infix expression has a variable access
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (varAccess != null) {
                    // Check if the null check is broken
                    if (infixExpression.hasDescendantMatchingXPath(".//InfixExpression//VariableAccess")) {
                        addViolation(data, (net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.Node) node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                    ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
                ASTInfixExpression childExpression = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = childExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("i")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }

        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNumericLiteral.class) || infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class) != null) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getImage().equals("list")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        else if (infixExpression != null && infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
            ASTInfixExpression nullCheck = infixExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class).getFirstParentOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (nullCheck != null && nullCheck.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
